<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хранить.html>храни́ть</a> (2851)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">хранити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xraniti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*xorniti</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хоронить.html>хорони́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xoronítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хранить.html>храни́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xranítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to keep (to maintain possession of), to preserve, to store
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:хранить.html>храни́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́ньги</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:банк.html>ба́нке</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xranítʹ</b> dénʹgi v bánke</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to keep one's money in a bank</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:хранить.html>храни́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тайна.html>та́йне</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xranítʹ</b> v tájne</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to keep (something) a secret</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to guard, to save, to protect
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:хранить.html>храни́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тебя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бог</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xraní</b> tebjá box</i> ― <span class="e-translation">God save you</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:храпеть.html>храпе́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xrapétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:захрапеть.html>захрапе́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">похрапе́ть</b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хребет.html>хребе́т</a> (4249)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*xrьbьtъ</i>. </p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хребет.html>хребе́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xrebét</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хребет.html>хребта́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хребет.html>хребты́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хребет.html>хребто́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>spine, spinal column, backbone <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">also figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>crest <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a wave or hill</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, ridge, range <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a chain of mountains</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">аля́скинский <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хребет.html>хребе́т</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Aljáskinskij <b>xrebét</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alaska_Range" class="extiw" title="w:Alaska Range">Alaska Range</a></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хрен.html>хрен</a> (2594)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">хрѣнъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xrěnŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>?, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*xrěnъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">horseradish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хрен.html>хрен</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xren</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хрен.html>хре́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хрен.html>хре́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хрен.html>хре́нов</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хреновый.html>хрено́вый</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> horseradish <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">plant, condiment</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">inanimate<span class="ib-comma">,</span> euphemistic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cock, dick <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">for vulgar idioms and literal uses of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хер.html>хер</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xer</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">хуй</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xuj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>Ни</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хрен.html>хрена́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>понима́ю</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:собрать.html>собра́ть</a>.</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">note the stress</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ni <b>xrená</b> ne ponimáju, kak éto sobrátʹ.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I understand bugger-all about how to put this together.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:какой.html>како́го</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хрен.html>хре́на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прийти.html>пришёл</a>?</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">note the stress</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Kakóvo <b>xréna</b> on prišól?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">What the fuck did he come for?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> old fart</li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0_2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства_2"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:хрен.html>хрен</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка). <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сочетание.html>сочета́ниях</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>ти́па</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хрен.html>хрен</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хрен.html>хрен</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хрен.html>хре́ну</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хрен.html>хрен</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ударение.html>ударе́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:падать.html>па́дать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:предлог.html>предло́г</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a> «<i><a href = vnd.unilang:хрен.html>хрен</a></i>» <a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́том</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:превращаться.html>превраща́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> клитику.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> знач. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:мужчина.html>мужчи́на</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склоняться.html>склоня́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:образец.html>образцу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>существи́тельных</a> (<span title="в винительном падеже"><a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кого́</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a>?</span> — <i><a href = vnd.unilang:хрен.html>хре́на</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:хрен.html>хренов</a></i>).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-хрен-</b>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хром.html>хром</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xrom</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хром.html>хро́ма</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хром.html>хро́мы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хромовый.html>хро́мов</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хромовый.html>хро́мовый</a></b>)

***хромать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хромать.html>хрома́ть</a> (14187)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хромой.html>хромо́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xromój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хромать.html>хрома́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xromátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to limp, to be lame
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:хромать.html>хрома́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:правый.html>пра́вую</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>но́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xromátʹ</b> na právuju nógu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be lame in the right leg</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be poor, to leave much to be desired, to be far from perfect, to not be up to standard
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хромать.html>хрома́ет</a></b> орфогра́фия</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó <b>xromájet</b> orfográfija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">his spelling is poor; his spelling leaves much to be desired</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b>хро<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:мать.html>ма́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — захромать, похромать.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-хром-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> chromic acid
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:хромовый.html>хро́мовое</a></b> дубле́ние</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xrómovoje</b> dublénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>chromic acid</b> tanning, <b>chrome</b> tanning</span></div></dd></dl></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хромой.html>хромо́й</a> (28093)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хромой.html>хромо́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xromój</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)хроме́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)хроме́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>lame, limping <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">unable to walk properly because of a problem with one's feet or legs</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>wobbly <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of furniture</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***хроника.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хроника.html>хро́ника</a> (15106)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Chronik</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">chronica</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">χρονικός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">khronikós</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">χρόνος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">khrónos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, of unknown origin.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

***хрусталь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хрусталь.html>хруста́ль</a> (13125)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Greek">Byzantine Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κρουστάλλιον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kroustállion</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a  diminutive form of <i class="Grek mention" lang="el">κρούσταλλον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="el-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kroústallon</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a variant of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Greek">Byzantine Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κρύσταλλον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krústallon</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, both ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κρύσταλλος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krústallos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Greek_language" class="extiw" title="w:Greek language">Greek</a></span> <i class="Grek mention" lang="el">κρούσταλλο</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="el-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kroústallo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The starting <i>х-</i> was possibly influenced by <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хрустеть.html>хрусте́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xrustétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хрусталь.html>хруста́ль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xrustálʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хрусталь.html>хрусталя́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хрусталь.html>хрустали́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хрусталь.html>хрустале́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>crystal <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">fine glassware, material used to make it</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>mineral
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горный.html>го́рный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хрусталь.html>хруста́ль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">górnyj xrustálʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">rock crystal</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
